","longBio":"Kalie joined KCRG-TV9 First Alert Weather Team in May of 2019. She comes from TV9's sister station in Shreveport, Louisiana where she was the weekend meteorologist.\n\nKalie is originally from Westfield, Indiana, and is a Hoosier at heart. She graduated from Ball State University in Muncie, Indiana in December 2017 with a degree in Meteorology & Climatology and is a proud Cardinal! While in college, she was a weather intern at WMC Action News 5 in Memphis, Tennessee as well as at WISH-TV in Indianapolis. Spending most of her life in the Midwest, she is used to all four seasons and all the wild weather that comes with Midwest living.\n\nWhile at Ball State, Kalie was involved all across campus. She held the Chief Weather Forecaster position for her campus’ TV station, NewsLink Indiana, her last semester, and forecasted for the station during her entire college career. She was also a proud co-founder of Ball State's only morning show, Waking Up with Cardinal Weather. During her freshman year of college, she was fortunate to head west and go storm chasing with a team from Ball State for two weeks and is a  proud member of Kappa Delta Sorority.\n\nOutside of the weather, Kalie is an avid sports fan. fellow First Alert Storm Team Meteorologist Kaj O’Mara. He went on to attend Valparaiso University in Valparaiso, Indiana, where he earned his Bachelor of Science in Meteorology in 2008.\n\nWhile at Valpo, Corey developed an interest in storm chasing by participating in two 11-day storm chase trips on the Great Plains, taking him and a team of 20 peers wherever the wind led them. He also got his first formal instruction on how to present a weather forecast for television from now-ABC’s Chief Meteorologist Ginger Zee.\n\nDuring college, Corey spent a summer as an intern in the KCRG-TV9 Weather Lab, working with Chief Meteorologist Joe Winters and the rest of the First Alert Storm Team to begin to hone his skills as a television meteorologist. After college, he returned to KCRG-TV9 for several years in a behind-the-scenes role, helping to conduct research and create weather graphics for use on-air.\n\nHaving lived in Eastern Iowa for nearly all of his life, Corey appreciates the variety of different weather conditions we experience throughout the year.
